country_event = {
	id = uk.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event uk.1"}
	title = "State of the Empire"
	desc = uk.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_british_inspect_troops
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { 
		set_country_flag = has_ministers
		hidden_effect = {
			IF = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				add_ideas = ENG_statute_autonomy2
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Interesting times ahead"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = uk.80 months = 3 }
			IF = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
					NOT = { has_country_flag = ENG_AI_CHOSEN }
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = uk.10000 hours = 1 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			IF = {
				limit = {
					BHU = { is_ai = yes }
				}
				BHU = { country_event = { id = uk.50000 days = 1 } }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {	# - Empire Day
			ENG = { country_event = { id = ukflavour.50 months = 4 } }
			CAN = { country_event = { id = ukflavour.50 months = 4 } }
			NZL = { country_event = { id = ukflavour.50 months = 4 } }
			AST = { country_event = { id = ukflavour.50 months = 4 } }
			SAF = { country_event = { id = ukflavour.50 months = 4 } }
		}
		hidden_effect = {	# - Empire Games '38
			country_event = { id = ukflavour.20 months = 26 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {	# - London Economic Conference
			#country_event = { id = uk.120 months = 24 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {	# - Anglo-American Conference
			#country_event = { id = nato.1 months = 10 }
			#USA = { country_event = { id = nato.1 months = 10 } }
		}
	}
}

add_namespace = ukbw

country_event = {
	id = uk.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event uk.2"}
	title = "London Stock Market Crash"
	desc = uk.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ENG
		date > 1936.9.1
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = FRA
			has_war_with = GER
			has_war_with = ITA
			has_war_with = JAP
			has_war_with = USA
			has_war_with = SOV
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "My God!"
		add_political_power = -50
		add_ideas = ENG_bw
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = ENG_stock_crash
			#complete_national_focus = ENG_black_wed 	##### THIS CRASHES THE GAME UNLESS PLAYER CURRENTLY RESEARCHING ANOTHER FOCUS
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = bw_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = bw_tt2
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					exists = yes
				}
				news_event = {
					id = worldnews.2 days = 1
				}
			}
			IRQ = { country_event = { id = irq.10 } }
      EGY = { country_event = { id = egypt.1 } }
			RAJ = { 
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = IMP_bw
					days = 365
				}
			}
			NFL = { 
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = IMP_bw
					days = 365
				}
			}
			AST = { 
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = IMP_bw
					days = 365
				}
			}
			NZL = { 
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = IMP_bw
					days = 365
				}
			}
			JAP = {
				news_event = { id = jap.9 }
			}
			SIA = {
				country_event = { id = siambw.1 }
			}
      ARB = {
        country_event = { id = arabia.11 days = 1 }
      }
			PHI = {
				country_event = { id = philippines.19 days = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ukbw.6
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukbw.6"}
	title = "Successful Policies"
	desc = ukbw.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference

	trigger = {
		tag = ENG
		OR = {
			has_idea = ENG_bw
			has_idea = ENG_bwa1
			has_idea = ENG_bwa2
			has_idea = ENG_bwa3
			has_idea = ENG_bwa4
			has_idea = ENG_bws1
			has_idea = ENG_bws2
			has_idea = ENG_bws3
			has_idea = ENG_bws4
			has_idea = ENG_bws5
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 24 }
	
	option = {
		name = "A good sign"
		add_political_power = 50
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_conservative
				social_conservative < 50
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_liberal
				social_liberal < 50
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				social_democrat < 50
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
				paternal_autocrat < 50
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				authoritarian_democrat < 50
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {

country_event = {
	id = uk.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event uk.3"}
	title = "A Peaceful Ending at Midnight"
	desc = uk.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_europe_funeral
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ENG
		date > 1936.1.20
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "More than a King, a father of a great family."
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = kgv_dead
			retire_character = ENG_George_V
      add_country_leader_role = {
        character = ENG_King_Edward_VIII
        promote_leader = yes
        country_leader = {
          desc = "POLITICS_ENG_EDWARD_VIII_DESC"
          ideology = vanguardist_subtype
          traits = { meddler charismatic }
        }
      }
      add_country_leader_role = {
        character = ENG_King_Edward_VIII
        promote_leader = yes
        country_leader = {
          desc = "POLITICS_ENG_EDWARD_VIII_DESC"

          traits = { meddler charismatic }
        }
      }

          desc = "POLITICS_ENG_EDWARD_VIII_DESC"

          traits = { meddler charismatic }
        }
      }
      add_country_leader_role = {
        character = ENG_King_Edward_VIII
        promote_leader = yes
        country_leader = {
          desc = "POLITICS_ENG_EDWARD_VIII_DESC"
          ideology = social_liberal_subtype
          traits = { meddler charismatic }
        }
      }

          desc = "POLITICS_ENG_EDWARD_VIII_DESC"

        }
      }

        character = ENG_King_Edward_VIII

			}
		}

###########################
# - Assassination/Survival of Edward VIII 
###########################

country_event = {
	id = uk.400
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event uk.400"}
	title = "The King's Commands"
	desc = uk.400.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "The King commands and we obey"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = avenging1776
				add = -50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = challengefrance
				add = 50
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { 
			country_event = { id = uk.4 days = 15 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Maintain the number of bodyguards nearby, whether he likes it or not"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = avenging1776
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = challengefrance
				add = -50
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { 
			country_event = { id = uk.5 days = 15 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = uk.4
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event uk.4"}
	title = "King Edward VIII assassinated"
	desc = uk.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_funeral
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Whatever the future brings, Britain will survive!"
		add_political_power = -100
		add_stability = -0.1
		hidden_effect = {
			retire_character = ENG_King_Edward_VIII
      add_country_leader_role = {

		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = uk.148 days = 7 }
			set_country_flag = mosley_in_power
			load_focus_tree = british_focus_mos
			IF = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						libertarian_socialist < 20
						libertarian_socialist > 10
					}
				}
				add_popularity = { ideology = libertarian_socialist popularity = 0.10 }
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					libertarian_socialist < 10
				}
				add_popularity = { ideology = libertarian_socialist popularity = 0.30 }
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						libertarian_socialist < 30
						libertarian_socialist > 20
					}
				}
				add_popularity = { ideology = libertarian_socialist popularity = 0.10 }
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
        character = ENG_Jock_Haston
        promote_leader = yes
        country_leader = {
          ideology = vanguardist_subtype
          traits = {}
        }
      }
      add_country_leader_role = {
        character = ENG_Arthur_MacManus
        promote_leader = yes
        country_leader = {
          ideology = collectivist_subtype
          traits = {}
        }
      }
      add_country_leader_role = {
        character = ENG_Oswald_Mosley
        promote_leader = yes
        country_leader = {
          ideology = libertarian_socialist_subtype
          traits = {}
        }
      }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ukf.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukf.1"}
	title = "The Arabian Peninsula"
	desc = ukf.1.d
	picture = report_event_europe_funeral
 
    fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
 
    #option = {
       # name = "Establish the Anglo-Arabian Oil Company"
		#ai_chance = {
			#base = 0
		#}
		#country_event = { id = ukf.2 days = 1 }
		#ARB = { country_event = { id = ukf.2 } }
    #}
	
	option = {
        name = "Justify a military incursion into the country"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ENG_c_imperial
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = RAS }
			create_wargoal = {
				target = RAS
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = ARB }
			create_wargoal = {
				target = ARB
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = SAU }
			create_wargoal = {
				target = SAU
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
    }
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ENG_c_imperial
		}
        name = "Forget diplomacy, crush them!"
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = RAS }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = RAS
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = ARB }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ARB
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = SAU }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ARB
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
    }
}

# - Channel Execises (ukf.70-ukf.81)

country_event = {
	id = ukf.70
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukf.70"}
	title = "Channel Exercises"
	desc = ukf.70.d
	picture = report_event_merchant_ship_01
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = ENG
		is_puppet = no
		has_war = no
		has_navy_size = { size > 100 }
		date > 1939.1.1
		OR = {
			has_completed_focus = ENG_national_effort
			has_completed_focus = ENG_end_austerity
			has_completed_focus = ENG_liberate_markets
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 30 }
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Instruct the Admiralty to move forward with the exercises"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = challengefrance
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = capesingapore
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = isoimpfed
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = avenging1776
				add = -50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = reformentente
				add = -50
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			IF = {
				limit = {
					FRA = { 
						exists = yes
						has_war = no
						NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
					}
				}
				FRA = { country_event = { id = ukf.71 days = 7 } }
				else = {
					country_event = { id = ukf.72 days = 14 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "There's no need for this"
		add_political_power = 100
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = challengefrance
				add = -50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = capesingapore
				add = -50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = isoimpfed
				add = -50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = avenging1776
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = reformentente
				add = 50
			}
		}
	}
}

		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = SCW_SPM_no_support_2
			}
			remove_ideas = SCW_SPM_no_support_2
		}
	}

			}
			POR = { country_event = { id = ukf.2002 days = 1 } }
		}
		set_country_flag = naval_conf
		set_country_flag = { flag = lnt_members value = 0 }
	}
}

# - London Naval Treaty membership checker

country_event = {
	id = ukf.2500
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukf.2500"}
	title = "London Naval Treaty Membership"
	desc = ukf.2500.d
	picture = report_event_merchant_ship_01
	
	fire_only_once = no	#why?
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = ENG
		has_country_flag = naval_conf
		AND = {
			has_country_flag = { flag = lnt_members value > 1 }
			has_country_flag = { flag = lnt_members value < 4 }
		}
		NOT = { has_idea = ENG_lnt1 }
		NOT = { has_idea = ENG_lnt2 }
		NOT = { has_idea = ENG_lnt3 }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "The London Naval Treaty ensures naval security"
		add_ideas = ENG_lnt1
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_puppet_of = ENG
			}
			add_ideas = IMP_lnt
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ukf.2501
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukf.2501"}
	title = "London Naval Treaty Membership"
	desc = ukf.2500.d
	picture = report_event_merchant_ship_01
	
	fire_only_once = no
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = ENG
		has_country_flag = naval_conf
		AND = {
			has_country_flag = { flag = lnt_members value > 3 }
			has_country_flag = { flag = lnt_members value < 6 }
		}
		NOT = { has_idea = ENG_lnt2 }
		NOT = { has_idea = ENG_lnt3 }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "The London Naval Treaty ensures naval security"
		swap_ideas = { remove_idea = ENG_lnt1 add_idea = ENG_lnt2 }
	}
}

	title = "London Naval Treaty Membership"
	desc = ukf.2500.d
	picture = report_event_merchant_ship_01
	
	fire_only_once = no
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = ENG
		has_country_flag = naval_conf
		has_country_flag = { flag = lnt_members value > 5 }
		NOT = { has_idea = ENG_lnt3 }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "The London Naval Treaty ensures naval security"
		swap_ideas = { remove_idea = ENG_lnt2 add_idea = ENG_lnt3 }
	}
}

country_event = {		# - France
	id = ukf.5000
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukf.5000"}
	title = "The Second Great War"
	desc = ukf.5000.d
	picture = report_event_merchant_ship_01
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

    fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "We cannot allow France to fall to the Germans, we must involve ourselves directly"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = reformentente
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = capesingapore
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war = yes
				add = -100
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			GER = { NOT = { has_idea = ENG_jutpact } }
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = GER
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = isolation
			}
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = isolation add_idea = civilian_economy }
		}
		add_political_power = 100
		set_country_flag = decided_gw2
		set_country_flag = gw2intervention
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Send the French equipment and ''volunteers''"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = capesingapore
				add = 25
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = reformentente
				add = -50
			}
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_1 amount = -10000 producer = ENG }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = support_equipment amount = -500 producer = ENG }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = artillery_equipment_1 amount = -500 producer = ENG }
		add_manpower = -50000
		FRA = { country_event = { id = ukf.5001 } }
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = isolation
			}
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = isolation add_idea = civilian_economy }
		}
		set_country_flag = decided_gw2
		set_country_flag = gw2intervention
		hidden_effect = {
			IF = {
				limit = {
					GER = { NOT = { has_idea = ENG_jutpact } }
				}
				country_event = { id = ukf.5002 days = 30 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "We have no interest in this right now"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = avenging1776
				add = 100
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = challengefrance
				add = 100
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = isoimpfed
				add = 100
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = capesingapore
				add = 25
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war = yes
				add = 100
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = deciding_gw2
	}
}

				ENG = { has_country_flag = indust37 }
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = IMP_workshop
				days = 180
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				ENG = { has_country_flag = infra37 }
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = IMP_infrastructure
				days = 180
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				ENG = { has_country_flag = milbase37 }
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = IMP_milbase
				days = 180
			}
		}
	}
}

# - Future of the Empire
# - Status Quo

country_event = {
	id = emp.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event emp.2"}
	title = "Britain pursues Imperial Status Quo"
	desc = emp.2.d
	picture = report_event_generic_conference
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			tag = CAN
		}
		name = "This is unacceptable!"
		ENG = { country_event = { id = emp.3 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				original_tag = RAJ
				ENG = { has_country_flag = india_truce }
			}
		}
		name = "This will surely only add fuel to the rebellion."
		hidden_effect = {
			IF = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						ENG = { has_country_flag = india_truce }
						ENG = { NOT = { has_country_flag = capesingapore } }
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = emp.8 months = 1 }
			}
			country_event = { id = emp.8 months = 1 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					tag = CAN 
					AND = {
						original_tag = RAJ
						ENG = { has_country_flag = india_truce }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = "The Status Quo ensures stability at least."
	}
}

			#-CAN MODIFIERS
			modifier = {
				original_tag = CAN
				add = 25
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					original_tag = CAN
					has_opinion = { target = ENG value < 0 }
				}
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					original_tag = CAN
					has_opinion = { target = ENG value > 49 }
				}
				add = -25
			}
			#-AST MODIFIERS
			modifier = {
				original_tag = AST
				add = 20
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					original_tag = AST
					has_opinion = { target = ENG value < 0 }
				}
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					original_tag = AST
					has_opinion = { target = ENG value > 49 }
				}
				add = -25
			}
			#-NZL MODIFIERS
			modifier = {
				original_tag = NZL
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					original_tag = NZL
					has_opinion = { target = ENG value < 0 }
				}
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					original_tag = NZL
					has_opinion = { target = ENG value > 49 }
				}
				add = -25
			}
			#-RAJ MODIFIER
			modifier = {
				original_tag = RAJ
				add = 50
			}
			#-SAF MODIFIERS
			modifier = {
				original_tag = SAF
				add = 45
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					original_tag = SAF
					has_opinion = { target = ENG value < 0 }
				}
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					original_tag = SAF
					has_opinion = { target = ENG value > 49 }
				}
				add = -25
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = rejects_federation
		IF = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = CAN
			}
			ENG = { country_event = { id = emp.16 days = 1 } }
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = AST
			}
			ENG = { country_event = { id = emp.17 days = 4 } }
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = SAF
			}
			ENG = { country_event = { id = emp.18 days = 2 } }
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = RAJ
			}
			ENG = { country_event = { id = emp.19 days = 3 } }
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = NZL
			}
			ENG = { country_event = { id = emp.20 days = 5 } }
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = NFL
			}
			ENG = { country_event = { id = emp.200 days = 6 } }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = emp.16
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event emp.16"}
	title = "Canadian Response"
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			CAN = { has_country_flag = accepts_federation }
		}
		text = "The Canadian Government has responded to our call for an Imperial Federation of the Empire positively, with a surprising agreement being formed over the issue."
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			CAN = { has_country_flag = rejects_federation }
		}
		text = "Unsurprisingly the Canadian Government has rejected our proposal for an Imperial Federation between our nations."
	}
	picture = report_event_generic_conference
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			CAN = { has_country_flag = accepts_federation }
		}
		name = "Their agreement will assist us greatly."
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			CAN = { has_country_flag = rejects_federation }
		}
		name = "We must convince them over the next few years."
	}	
}

				}

			}
		}

##### Returning Raj Land #####

country_event = {
	id = emp.45
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event emp.45"}
	title = "Return of the Raj"
	desc = "With our rule in India restored to yet another bit of land on the Indian sub-continent the time has arrived for us to return it to its rightful owner and our loyal puppet."
	picture = report_event_generic_conference
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = ENG
		RAJ = { is_puppet_of = ENG }
		OR = {	# - I really wish there was an easier way of doing this
			controls_state = 423
			controls_state = 425
			controls_state = 424
			controls_state = 427
			controls_state = 429
			controls_state = 809
			controls_state = 814
			controls_state = 426
			controls_state = 436
			controls_state = 812
			controls_state = 437
			controls_state = 435
			controls_state = 431
			controls_state = 430
			controls_state = 432
			controls_state = 434
			controls_state = 438
			controls_state = 884
			controls_state = 433
			controls_state = 428
			controls_state = 443
			controls_state = 444
			controls_state = 439
			controls_state = 440
			controls_state = 883
			controls_state = 441
			controls_state = 445
			controls_state = 442
			controls_state = 811
		}
		has_war = no 
		is_ai = no
		has_country_flag = reconquering_india
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }
	
	option = {
		name = "The Raj shall be restored to its former glory"
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				is_core_of = RAJ
			}
			RAJ = { transfer_state = PREV }
			IF = {		# Hopefully this will stop Raj becoming stupidly OP
				limit = {
					industrial_complex > 3
					industrial_complex < 8
				}
				remove_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 3 }
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					industrial_complex > 8		# why
				}
				remove_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 5 }
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					arms_factory > 3
					arms_factory < 8
				}
				remove_building = { type = arms_factory level = 3 }
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					arms_factory > 8		# why
				}
				remove_building = { type = arms_factory level = 5 }
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					dockyard > 3
					dockyard < 8
				}
				remove_building = { type = dockyard level = 3 }
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					dockyard > 8		# why
				}
				remove_building = { type = dockyard level = 5 }
			}
		}
	}
}

		text = emp.51a.d
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { NOT = { CAN = { has_country_flag = accepts_federation } } }
		text = emp.51b.d
	}
	picture = report_event_generic_conference
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

		trigger = { 
			CAN = { has_country_flag = accepts_federation } 
		}
		name = "Excellent"
	}

			NOT = { CAN = { has_country_flag = accepts_federation } }
		}
		name = "Let them go!"
		end_puppet = CAN
		remove_from_faction = CAN
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { CAN = { has_country_flag = accepts_federation } }

		name = "We will restore order to our territory!"
		end_puppet = CAN
		remove_from_faction = CAN
		declare_war_on = {
			type = puppet_wargoal_focus
			target = CAN
		}
	}
}

		}

	desc = ukadm.17.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_british_inspect_troops
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = ENG
		has_war = yes
		OR = {
			has_army_experience > 49
			has_air_experience > 49
		}
		has_country_flag = ENG_rn_primacy
		has_war = no 
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Unfortunate, but not unexpected."
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_army_experience > 49
			}
			army_experience = -50
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_army_experience > 39
				has_army_experience < 50
			}
			army_experience = -40
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_army_experience > 29
				has_army_experience < 40
			}
			army_experience = -30
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_army_experience > 19
				has_army_experience < 30
			}
			army_experience = -20
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_army_experience > 9
				has_army_experience < 20
			}
			army_experience = -10
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_air_experience > 49
			}
			air_experience = -50
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_air_experience > 39
				has_air_experience < 50
			}
			air_experience = -40
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_air_experience > 29
				has_air_experience < 40
			}
			air_experience = -30
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_air_experience > 19
				has_air_experience < 30
			}
			air_experience = -20
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_air_experience > 9
				has_air_experience < 20
			}
			air_experience = -10
		}
	}
}
